OUTPUT: >--+--------------------------------------+-------------------->< -

OUTPUT:                        '-Yes---------' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: A (at least one of these parameters must be specified) -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: |--+-----------------------------+------------------------------> -
OUTPUT:    |  (2)                        | -
OUTPUT:    '--------STGPool--=--poolname-' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: >--+----------------------------------+-------------------------> -
OUTPUT:    |  (2)          (3)                | -
OUTPUT:    '--------RETSet-------=--retset_id-' -

OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Notes: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 1. The READCLOUDDATA parameter applies only to cloud volumes. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 2. You cannot specify a volume name if you specify a storage pool -
OUTPUT:    name, retention set ID, FROMDATE, or TODATE. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 3. You can filter a list of volumes that contain data for a -
OUTPUT:    retention set by specifying the RETSET parameter with one or -
OUTPUT:    more of the following parameters: STGPOOL, FROMDATE, and -
OUTPUT:    TODATE. -

OUTPUT:    you specify the COMPRESS parameter in the BACKUP DB command, -
OUTPUT:    it overrides any COMPRESS parameter value that is set in the -
OUTPUT:    SET DBRECOVERY command. Otherwise, the value that is set in -
OUTPUT:    the SET DBRECOVERY command is the default. -

OUTPUT:    specify the IDENTITY parameter. -

OUTPUT:                       .-,----------. -
OUTPUT:              (1)      V            | -
OUTPUT: >--HLAddress-------=----ip_address-+-?PEA_file------------------> -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:    .-MINCAPacity--=--100M-.  .-MOUNTLimit--=--1------. -
OUTPUT: >--+----------------------+--+-----------------------+--------->< -
OUTPUT:    '-MINCAPacity--=--size-'  '-MOUNTLimit--=--number-' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Notes: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 1. For each Centera device class, you must specify one or more IP -
OUTPUT:    addresses. However, a Pool Entry Authorization (PEA) file name -
OUTPUT:    and path are optional, and up to one PEA file specification -
OUTPUT:    can follow the IP addresses. Use the "?" character to separate -
OUTPUT:    the PEA file name and path from the IP addresses. -
OUTPUT:  -
Next: Help for: 3.17.12.6

OUTPUT: Syntax -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: >>-DEFine DEVclass--device_class_name--DEVType--=--CLOUD--------> -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: >--CONNection--=--connection_name-------------------------------> -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:    .-CLOUDSTORAGEClass--=--Default--------------------. -
OUTPUT: >--+--------------------------------------------------+-------->< -
OUTPUT:    '-CLOUDSTORAGEClass--=--+-Default----------------+-' -
OUTPUT:                            +-AUTOmaticvendortiering-+ -
OUTPUT:                            +-NEARLINE---------------+ -
OUTPUT:                            +-GLACIER----------------+ -
OUTPUT:                            +-DEEPGLACIER------------+ -
OUTPUT:                            +-ARchive----------------+ -
OUTPUT:                            +-ACCARchive-------------+ -
OUTPUT:                            +-COLDLINE---------------+ -
OUTPUT:                            '-GLACIER_IR-------------' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Restriction: The GLACIER, DEEPGLACIER, ARchive, and ACCARchive -
OUTPUT: storage classes are used for retention storage pools. These -
OUTPUT: classes must not be used for other types of data, like database -
OUTPUT: backup or container storage pools. If the ARchive and ACCARchive -
OUTPUT: values are used, then the bucket must not be shared with other -
OUTPUT: types of data. The bucket must only be used by the associated -
OUTPUT: retention storage pool. -
OUTPUT:  -
Next: Help for: 3.17.12.7

OUTPUT:    driver. -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT:    generation LTO drives and media. -

OUTPUT: >--+-------------------------------------------+--------------->< -
OUTPUT:    |                     (3)                   | -
OUTPUT:    '-CLEANFREQuency--=-------+-NONE----------+-' -
OUTPUT:                              |          (4)  | -
OUTPUT:                              +-ASNEEDED------+ -
OUTPUT:                              '-gigabytes-----' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Notes: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 1. The ELEMENT parameter is only necessary for drives in SCSI -
OUTPUT:    libraries when the drive type is a network attached SCSI (NAS) -
OUTPUT:    drive. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 2. ACSDRVID is required for drives in ACSLS libraries. This -
OUTPUT:    parameter is not valid for non-ACSLS libraries. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 3. The CLEANFREQUENCY parameter is valid only for drives in SCSI -
OUTPUT:    libraries. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 4. The CLEANFREQUENCY=ASNEEDED parameter value does not work for -
OUTPUT:    all tape drives. For more information, see the parameter -
OUTPUT:    description. -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT: Syntax and parameter descriptions are available for the following -
OUTPUT: path types. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Tip: To display information about a specific command in the -
OUTPUT: following list, type HELP followed by the topic number for that -
OUTPUT: command. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  3.17.26.1 DEFINE PATH (Define a path when the destination is a -
OUTPUT:    drive) -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  3.17.26.2 DEFINE PATH (Define a path when the destination is a -
OUTPUT:    library) -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  3.17.26.3 DEFINE PATH (Define a path when the destination is a -
OUTPUT:    ZOSMEDIA library) -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: For detailed and current device support information, see the -
OUTPUT: Supported Devices website for your operating system: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:    http://www.ibm.com/software/sysmgmt/products/support/IBM_TSM_Supported_Devices_for_Linux.html -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Related commands -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Table 95. Commands related to DEFINE PATH -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | Command                       | Description                   | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | DEFINE DATAMOVER              | Defines a data mover to the   | -
OUTPUT: |                               | IBM Spectrum Protect server.  | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | DEFINE DRIVE                  | Assigns a drive to a library. | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | DEFINE LIBRARY                | Defines an automated or       | -
OUTPUT: |                               | manual library.               | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | DELETE PATH                   | Deletes a path from a source  | -
OUTPUT: |                               | to a destination.             | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | PERFORM LIBACTION             | Defines all drives and paths  | -
OUTPUT: |                               | for a library.                | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | QUERY PATH                    | Displays information about    | -
OUTPUT: |                               | the path from a source to a   | -
OUTPUT: |                               | destination.                  | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | UPDATE DATAMOVER              | Changes the definition for a  | -
OUTPUT: |                               | data mover.                   | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | UPDATE PATH                   | Changes the attributes        | -
OUTPUT: |                               | associated with a path.       | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -

OUTPUT: Notes: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 1. The filespace_name can correspond to a file space on a -
OUTPUT:    backup-archive client or to an IBM Spectrum Protect for -
OUTPUT:    Virtual Environments virtual machine. To specify the virtual -
OUTPUT:    machine, use either the virtual machine name or the -
OUTPUT:    corresponding file space name. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 2. If you specify a file space name, you can specify only one -
OUTPUT:    fully qualified node name. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 3. To create a retroactive retention set that collects past data -
OUTPUT:    by one-time retention rule, you must define the retention rule -
OUTPUT:    with STARTTIME and STARTDATE parameter values. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 4. To specify the HOLD and HOLDREASON parameters, you must also -
OUTPUT:    specify FREQUENCY=ONETIME. -

OUTPUT: Syntax for command routing, server monitoring, and -

OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Command routing -

OUTPUT: *  Status monitoring of remote servers -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Alert monitoring of remote servers -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Server-to-server export -

OUTPUT: administrator who is issuing the command. -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT:    definitions. -

OUTPUT:    to storage agent definitions. -

OUTPUT:    operating systems. -

OUTPUT: Notes: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 1. The RECLAMATIONTYPE=SNAPLOCK setting is valid only for storage -
OUTPUT:    pools that are defined to servers that are enabled for IBM -
OUTPUT:    Spectrum Protect for Data Retention. The storage pool must be -
OUTPUT:    assigned to a FILE device class, and the directories that are -
OUTPUT:    specified in the device class must be NetApp SnapLock volumes. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 2. The values NETAPPDUMP, CELERRADUMP, and NDMPDUMP are not valid -
OUTPUT:    for storage pools that are defined with a FILE device class. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 3. This parameter is valid only for storage pools that are -
OUTPUT:    defined with a FILE device class. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 4. This parameter is available only when the value of the -
OUTPUT:    DEDUPLICATE parameter is YES. -
OUTPUT:  -

Next: Help for: 3.49.47

OUTPUT: Syntax -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: >>-Query MONITORSEttings--------------------------------------->< -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Display monitoring settings -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Display details about the monitoring settings. See Field -
OUTPUT: descriptions for more details. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: query monitorsettings -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Example output: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:                                 Monitor Status: On -
OUTPUT:              Status Refresh Interval (Minutes): 5 -
OUTPUT:                       Status Retention (Hours): 48 -
OUTPUT:                         Monitor Message Alerts: On -
OUTPUT:                Alert Update Interval (Minutes): 10 -
OUTPUT:                                 Alert to Email: On -
OUTPUT:           Send Alert Summary to Administrators: On -
OUTPUT:                       Alert from Email Address: DJADMIN@MYDOMAIN.COM -
OUTPUT:                                Alert SMTP Host: DJHOST.MYDOMAIN.COM -
OUTPUT:                                Alert SMTP Port: 25 -
OUTPUT:                Alert Active Duration (Minutes): 480 -
OUTPUT:              Alert Inactive Duration (Minutes): 480 -
OUTPUT:                Alert Closed Duration (Minutes): 60 -
OUTPUT:                               Monitoring Admin: ADMIN -
OUTPUT:                                Monitored Group: MONGROUP -
OUTPUT:                              Monitored Servers: SERVER2 -
OUTPUT:              At-Risk Interval for Applications: 24 -
OUTPUT:     Skipped files as At-Risk for Applications?: Yes -
OUTPUT:          At-Risk Interval for Virtual Machines: 24 -
OUTPUT: Skipped files as At-Risk for Virtual Machines?: Yes -
OUTPUT:                   At-Risk Interval for Systems: 24 -
OUTPUT:          Skipped files as At-Risk for Systems?: Yes -
OUTPUT:            At-Risk Interval for Object Clients: 24 -
OUTPUT:                          Deployment Repository: /source/packages/deploy -
OUTPUT:                    Maximum Deployment Packages: 4 -
OUTPUT:                     Deployment Package Manager: On -
OUTPUT:                         Security Notifications: On -
OUTPUT:   Security Notifications Last Update Date/Time: 12/05/2019 15:57:37 -
OUTPUT:       Security Notifications Last Update Admin: ADMIN1 -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Field descriptions -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Monitor Status -
OUTPUT:          Specifies whether alert monitoring on the server is -
OUTPUT:          enabled or disabled. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Status Refresh Interval (Minutes) -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the number of minutes between intervals that -
OUTPUT:          the monitoring server gathers event data. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Status Retention (Hours) -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the number of hours that status monitoring -
OUTPUT:          indicators are retained. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Monitor Message Alerts -
OUTPUT:          Specifies whether alerts are sent to administrators by -
OUTPUT:          email. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Alert Update Interval (Minutes) -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the length of time, in minutes, that the alert -
OUTPUT:          monitor waits before the alert is updated and pruned on -
OUTPUT:          the server. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Alert to Email -
OUTPUT:          Specifies whether alerts are sent to administrators by -
OUTPUT:          email. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Send Alert Summary to Administrators -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the administrators that receive a summary of -
OUTPUT:          existing alerts on the server in an email. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Alert from Email Address -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the email address of the sender. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Alert SMTP Host -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the Simple Mail Transfer Protocol (SMTP) host -
OUTPUT:          mail server that is used to send alerts by email. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Alert SMTP Port -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the SMTP mail server port that is used to send -
OUTPUT:          alerts by email. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Alert Active Duration (Minutes) -
OUTPUT:          Specifies how long, in minutes, an alert remains active. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Alert Inactive Duration (Minutes) -
OUTPUT:          Specifies how long, in minutes, an alert remains -
OUTPUT:          inactive. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Alert Closed Duration (Minutes) -
OUTPUT:          Specifies how long, in minutes, an alert remains closed -
OUTPUT:          before it is deleted from the server. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Monitoring Admin -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the name of the monitoring administrator that -
OUTPUT:          is used to connect to the servers in the monitored -
OUTPUT:          group. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Monitored Group -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the name of the monitored server group. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Monitored Servers -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the names of the servers in the monitored -
OUTPUT:          server group. The monitor settings might be different on -
OUTPUT:          each monitored server. If so, issue the query command -
OUTPUT:          for each server to display the monitoring settings. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: At-Risk Interval for Applications -
OUTPUT:          Specifies how long, in hours, an applications client can -
OUTPUT:          log no activity before it is considered at-risk. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Skipped files as At-Risk for Applications? -
OUTPUT:          Specifies that the server considers skipped files, by -
OUTPUT:          the client as a failure, and marks the client at-risk. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: At-Risk Interval for Virtual Machines -
OUTPUT:          Specifies how long, in hours, a virtual client can log -
OUTPUT:          no activity before it is considered at-risk. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Skipped files as At-Risk for Virtual Machines? -
OUTPUT:          Specifies that the server considers skipped files, by -
OUTPUT:          the client as a failure and marks the client at-risk. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: At-Risk Interval for Systems -
OUTPUT:          Specifies how long, in hours, a systems client can log -
OUTPUT:          no activity before it is considered at-risk. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Skipped files as At-Risk for Systems? -
OUTPUT:          Specifies that the server considers skipped files, by -
OUTPUT:          the client as a failure, and marks the client at-risk. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: At-Risk Interval for Object Clients: -
OUTPUT:          Specifies how long, in hours, an object client can log -
OUTPUT:          no activity before it is considered at-risk. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Deployment Repository -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the location where client deployment packages -
OUTPUT:          are downloaded, and the location of the storage volumes -
OUTPUT:          that are used for client deployment packages. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Maximum Deployment Packages -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the maximum number of client deployment -
OUTPUT:          packages that are stored in the deployment repository -
OUTPUT:          for each product version. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Deployment Package Manager -
OUTPUT:          Specifies whether the deployment package manager queries -
OUTPUT:          the download site for new deployment packages and -
OUTPUT:          downloads new packages as they become available. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Security Notifications -
OUTPUT:          Specifies whether security notifications are enabled. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Security Notifications Last Update Date/Time -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the date and time when the security -
OUTPUT:          notifications setting was last modified. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Security Notifications Last Update Admin -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the name of the administrator who most -
OUTPUT:          recently modified the security notifications setting. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Related commands -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT: information. For sample outputs for these query commands, see the -
OUTPUT: individual commands. -

OUTPUT: |                               | database.                     | -

OUTPUT: |                               | the database.                 | -

OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -

OUTPUT: |                               | management classes.           | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -
OUTPUT: | QUERY MONITORSETTINGS         | Displays information about    | -
OUTPUT: |                               | monitoring alerts and server  | -
OUTPUT: |                               | status settings.              | -
OUTPUT: +-------------------------------+-------------------------------+ -

OUTPUT: |                               | server options.               | -

OUTPUT: |                               | background processes.         | -

OUTPUT: |                               | node replication rules.       | -

OUTPUT:                         '-LDap--' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:                                (5) -
OUTPUT:    .-SSLrequired--=--DEFault--------. -
OUTPUT: >--+--------------------------------+---------------------------> -
OUTPUT:    '-SSLrequired--=--+-Yes--------+-' -
OUTPUT:                      +-No---------+ -
OUTPUT:                      +-DEFault----+ -
OUTPUT:                      '-SERVERonly-' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:    .-SESSIONSECurity--=--TRANSitional-----. -
OUTPUT: >--+--------------------------------------+---------------------> -
OUTPUT:    '-SESSIONSECurity--=--+-STRict-------+-' -
OUTPUT:                          '-TRANSitional-' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:    .-SPLITLARGEObjects--=--Yes-----. -
OUTPUT: >--+-------------------------------+----------------------------> -
OUTPUT:    '-SPLITLARGEObjects--=--+-Yes-+-' -
OUTPUT:                            '-No--' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:    .-MINIMUMExtentsize--=--50KB------. -
OUTPUT: >--+---------------------------------+------------------------->< -
OUTPUT:    '-MINIMUMExtentsize--=--+-50KB--+-' -
OUTPUT:                            +-250KB-+ -
OUTPUT:                            '-750KB-' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Notes: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 1. The PASSEXP command does not apply to administrators who -
OUTPUT:    authenticate with a Lightweight Directory Access Protocol -
OUTPUT:    (LDAP) directory server. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 2. The VALIDATEPROTOCOL parameter is deprecated. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 3. You can specify the BKREPLRULEDEFAULT, ARREPLRULEDEFAULT, or -
OUTPUT:    SPREPLRULEDEFAULT parameter only if you specify the REPLSTATE -
OUTPUT:    parameter. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 4. The default value can change if you issued the SET -
OUTPUT:    DEFAULTAUTHENTICATION command and specified LDAP. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 5. The SSLREQUIRED parameter is deprecated. -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT: clients to IBM Spectrum Protect -

Next: Help for: 3.69

OUTPUT: Syntax -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: For SELECT statement syntax and guidelines, search the Db2 -
OUTPUT: product information. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Important: The appropriate syntax for the timestamp Select -
OUTPUT: statement is: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: SELECT * FROM SUMMARY WHERE ACTIVTY='EXPIRATION' AND START_TIME -
OUTPUT: >'2009-05-10 00:00:00' AND START_TIME <'2009-05-11 23:23:23' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: List of examples -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: The SELECT command is used to customize a wide variety of -
OUTPUT: queries. To give you an idea of what you can do with the command, -
OUTPUT: this section includes many examples. There are, however, many -
OUTPUT: more possibilities. Query output is shown only for the more -
OUTPUT: complex commands to illustrate formatting. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: The following list summarizes the example SELECT commands: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List administrator user ID passwords that are authenticated -
OUTPUT:    with an external LDAP directory server -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List available tables -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List client nodes and administrative clients that are -
OUTPUT:    currently locked from server access -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List client nodes, administrative clients, and servers that -
OUTPUT:    are using transitional session security -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List client nodes and administrative clients that have not -
OUTPUT:    specified the correct password lately -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List nodes in the standard policy domain that are not -
OUTPUT:    associated with the daily backup schedule DAILYBACKUP -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List administrator user IDs that are designated as approval -
OUTPUT:    administrators -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List the administrators that have policy authority -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List type E (ERROR) or W (WARNING) messages that have been -
OUTPUT:    issued in the time period for which activity log records have -
OUTPUT:    been maintained -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List the administrative schedules that have been defined or -
OUTPUT:    altered by administrator JAKE -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List the relative administrative schedule priorities -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List the management classes that have an archive copy group -
OUTPUT:    with a retention period greater than 365 days -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List the client nodes that are in each policy domain -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Count how many files have been archived from each node -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  List the clients that are using space management -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Determine how many volumes would be reclaimed if the -
OUTPUT:    reclamation threshold is changed to 50 percent for storage -
OUTPUT:    pool TAPE -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Determine how many backup files would be affected for each -
OUTPUT:    node if the DAILY management class in the STANDARD policy -
OUTPUT:    domain is changed or deleted -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  For all active client sessions, determine how long have they -
OUTPUT:    been connected and their effective throughput in bytes per -
OUTPUT:    second -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Determine how long the current background processes have been -
OUTPUT:    running and determine their effective throughput in time and -
OUTPUT:    files per second -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Count the number of client nodes for each platform type -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Count the number of file spaces for each client node and list -
OUTPUT:    the client nodes in ascending order -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: *  Obtain statistical information for calculating the number of -
OUTPUT:    off-site volumes that have their space reclaimed during -
OUTPUT:    reclamation of a storage pool -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Field descriptions -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Tip: The following list describes fields that are typically -
OUTPUT: displayed in the output of SELECT commands for PVU estimates. The -
OUTPUT: displayed fields can vary, depending on the command that is -
OUTPUT: issued. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PRODUCT -
OUTPUT:          Rollup of license types into products at the level -
OUTPUT:          presented in the QUERY PVUESTIMATE command. Possible -
OUTPUT:          values are PRODEE, PROTBASIC, PRODDATARET, PRODMAIL, -
OUTPUT:          PRODDB, PRODSYSB, PRODSPACE, PRODSAN, PRODERP, or blank. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: LICENSE_NAME -
OUTPUT:          The license assigned to this node. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: NODE_NAME -
OUTPUT:          The node name. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: LAST_USED -
OUTPUT:          Date and time when the identified node last connected to -
OUTPUT:          the system under this license. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: TRYBUY -
OUTPUT:          Indication of whether try-and-buy mode is enabled. -
OUTPUT:          Possible values are TRUE or FALSE. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PROC_VENDOR -
OUTPUT:          Processor vendor name as reported by the client. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PROC_BRAND -
OUTPUT:          Processor brand name as reported by the client. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PROC_TYPE -
OUTPUT:          Processor type as reported by the client. This value -
OUTPUT:          also reflects the number of cores. Example values are -
OUTPUT:          1=SINGLE CORE, 2=DUO CORE, and 4=QUAD CORE. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PROC_MODEL -
OUTPUT:          Processor model as reported by the client. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PROC_COUNT -
OUTPUT:          Processor quantity. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: ROLE -
OUTPUT:          Node role. Possible values are CLIENT, SERVER, or OTHER. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: ROLE_OVERRIDE -
OUTPUT:          Override value specified in the UPDATE NODE command. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: ROLE_EFFECTIVE -
OUTPUT:          Actual role based on the values in the ROLE and -
OUTPUT:          ROLE_OVERRIDE fields. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: VALUE_UNITS -
OUTPUT:          Assigned processor value unit (PVU) for the processor. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PVU -
OUTPUT:          Calculated PVU value, as shown in the following formula: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          PVU per node = number of processors per node * processor type * pvu value -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          where the processor type represents the number of cores, -
OUTPUT:          and the pvu value is the value defined for the processor -
OUTPUT:          type in the IBM PVU table. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: VALUE_FROM_TABLE -
OUTPUT:          Flag that indicates whether the PVU was calculated based -
OUTPUT:          on the IBM PVU table. Possible values are YES or NO. If -
OUTPUT:          NO, a value of 100 is applied for each node defined as a -
OUTPUT:          server. If no role is defined for a node, the role of -
OUTPUT:          server is assumed for purposes of PVU calculation. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: SCAN_ERROR -
OUTPUT:          Flag that indicates whether license information was -
OUTPUT:          reported by client. Possible values are YES or NO. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: API_CLIENT -
OUTPUT:          Flag that indicates an API application. Possible values -
OUTPUT:          are YES or NO. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PVU_AGNOSTIC -
OUTPUT:          Flag indicating that the client version release level is -
OUTPUT:          earlier than IBM Spectrum Protect 6.3. If the version is -
OUTPUT:          earlier than 6.3, valid PVU metrics are not expected. -
OUTPUT:          Possible values are YES or NO. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: HYPERVISOR -
OUTPUT:          Name of the virtual machine software as reported by the -
OUTPUT:          client. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: GUID -
OUTPUT:          Globally Unique Identifier (GUID) of the computer where -
OUTPUT:          the node is located. The GUID is obtained from the node -
OUTPUT:          table. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: VERSION -
OUTPUT:          Version of client. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: RELEASE -
OUTPUT:          Release of client. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: LEVEL -
OUTPUT:          Level of client. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: OBJECT_AGENT -
OUTPUT:          Specifies whether the server is an object agent. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: BUCKETNAME -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the name of the bucket. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: VENDOR_D -
OUTPUT:          Processor vendor display value from the PVU table. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: BRAND_D -
OUTPUT:          Processor brand display value from the PVU table. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: TYPE_D -
OUTPUT:          Processor type display value from the PVU table. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: MODEL_D -
OUTPUT:          Processor model display value from the PVU table. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: PRODUCT_D -
OUTPUT:          Product display value from the PVU table. The following -
OUTPUT:          values are possible: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect Extended Edition -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect for Data Retention -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect for SAN -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect for Space Management -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect for Mail -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect for Databases -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect for Enterprise Resource Planning -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  IBM Spectrum Protect for System Backup and Recovery -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          *  Blank -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: ANS8002I Highest return code was 0. -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT:    command. -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT:    changing the authentication method from LDAP to LOCAL. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 3. The SYNCldapdelete parameter applies only if an administrator -
OUTPUT:    that is authenticating to an LDAP directory server reverts to -
OUTPUT:    local authentication. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 4. The SSLREQUIRED parameter is deprecated. -
OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT:    specify MFAREQUIRED=NO. When you update your own administrator -
OUTPUT:    ID, you cannot specify MFAREQUIRED=NO. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 6. The SHAREDSECRET parameter can be specified only if you -
OUTPUT:    specified MFAREQUIRED=YES. -

OUTPUT:                            '-GLACIER_IR-------------' -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Restriction: The GLACIER, DEEPGLACIER, ARchive, and ACCARchive -
OUTPUT: storage classes are used for retention storage pools. These -
OUTPUT: classes must not be used for other types of data, like database -
OUTPUT: backup or container storage pools. If the ARchive and ACCARchive -
OUTPUT: values are used, then the bucket must not be shared with other -
OUTPUT: types of data. The bucket must only be used by the associated -
OUTPUT: retention storage pool. -
OUTPUT:  -
Next: Help for: 3.78.11.7

OUTPUT:  -

OUTPUT:    however, IBM Tape Device drivers do not. In the event of an -
OUTPUT:    issue with the LTO-2 drive, the preferred corrective action is -
OUTPUT:    to upgrade your tape drive hardware to a higher generation -
OUTPUT:    drive, then install the latest version of the device driver. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 2. You cannot specify DRIVEENCRYPTION=ON if your drives are using -
OUTPUT:    WORM (write once, read many) media. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 3. Drive encryption is supported only for LTO-4 and higher -
OUTPUT:    generation LTO drives and media. -

OUTPUT:                          |             (4)                | -
OUTPUT:                          +-ACTIVE_DATA--------------------+ -
OUTPUT:                          +-ALL_DATA_HIGH_PRIORITY---------+ -

OUTPUT:                      +-DISabled--+ -

OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 1. You cannot specify a file space identifier (FSID) if you use -
OUTPUT:    wildcard characters for the client node name. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 2. You can specify each rule only once. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 3. You must specify either the REPLRULE or the REPLSTATE -
OUTPUT:    parameter on this command. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 4. The ACTIVE_DATA and ACTIVE_DATA_HIGH_PRIORITY rules are valid -
OUTPUT:    only if you specify DATATYPE=BACKUP. -

OUTPUT: Notes: -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 1. The filespace_name can correspond to a file space on a -
OUTPUT:    backup-archive client or to an IBM Spectrum Protect for -
OUTPUT:    Virtual Environments virtual machine. If you specify a -
OUTPUT:    filespace name, you can specify only one fully qualified node -
OUTPUT:    name. To specify the virtual machine, use either the virtual -
OUTPUT:    machine name or the corresponding filespace name. This -
OUTPUT:    restriction is relevant for both the add client and remove -
OUTPUT:    client actions. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: 2. To specify the HOLD and HOLDREASON parameters, -
OUTPUT:    FREQUENCY=ONETIME must be specified. -

OUTPUT: Syntax -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: >>-DBDIAGPATHFSTHreshold--percent------------------------------>< -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Parameter -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: percent -
OUTPUT:          Specifies the percentage of available space in the file -
OUTPUT:          system. Valid values are in the range 0 - 100. The -
OUTPUT:          default is 20. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:          Tip: For best results, do not set a low or high value -
OUTPUT:          for the percent parameter. A low value might cause the -
OUTPUT:          file system to become full before you can correct the -
OUTPUT:          issue. A full file system might corrupt the server -
OUTPUT:          database. A high value might result in many ANR1545W -
OUTPUT:          messages in the server activity log. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Example -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: Set the threshold value to 10%. -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: setopt DBDIAGPATHFSTH 10 -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT:  -
OUTPUT: ANS8002I Highest return code was 0. -
OUTPUT:  -
